< review>
I've only really worked with Bredan. He is very helpful with everything that I've ever needed. I only met Georgetta today but she seemed very pleasant. The only downfall of this storage facility is that you can't get into the gates after 7 pm and the outside doors are always open so there's no telling if mice or bugs are getting into your storage. I haven't seen any droppings but I did find a few daddy long legs. I accidently locked myself out of the gates with some stuff outside of my storage. The grounds and storage unit are very clean, my storage unit is carpeted which I really like.  All in all great customer service a little pricy but well worth it for hvac climate control.</review>

My second (and last) experience was in the surgical operations ward. I was told I would receive phone calls about pre-op Covid test, pre-op patient information interview, and a final call as to my operation time. I received NONE of these calls, I had to initiate every call in order to get the information. I provided feedback to the chief of surgical operation, who passed me along to the head of Human Resources, who passed me along to the next. I finally called the CEO directly in order to inform him of the terrible experience - he brushed me off and asked ‚Äúwhat do you want me to do about it?‚Äù. Zero empathy for someone receiving no attention from the people I am trusting to operate on me under anesthesia. The operation time finally came around, and even though I put up a major fuss about the low quality of service I had received, the operators still managed to show no regard for my experience - chipping my front tooth during the operation. Not only did they disregard my well being, they GAVE me an entirely different patients medical information, pictures, and diagnosis. Huge HIPAA violation. RIDICULOUS. After calling to inform them of the mishap, the only response from Casa Colina was a call from the head of compliance. < Text>
this place seems to be a typical coffee house vibe with some board games, a few tables and a couch to hang out at. They have a few different kinds of items on their menu such as acai bowls, juices, smoothies, and milk teas with boba.

Me and my friend tried the jasmine milk tea and the regular milk tea with boba. There's a lot of boba places near me so compared to them, pulp juice bar didn't have the best boba i've ever had just because the boba itself was pretty hard that we couldn't even eat it. I think out of the two options, both me and my friend would definitely prefer the jasmine milk tea over the regular one.

This place is definitely insta worthy and honestly it was pretty cool drinking something out of a pouch, its like an adult version of the capri sun! Next time I go I'll try one of their juices for sure.<//Text>

<rating>5<//rating>< review>
Excellent restaurant, unfortunately only takeout at present. Our take out dinner a couple of nights ago was very good. Probably the best lamb I have eaten in a very long time. The owner ws very pleasant and helpful. It's slightly on the pricier side, but typical of Carmel pricing, however the food was absolutely worth it. We will order again from them before we leave Carmel in a few days.

4/10/21 update.

Had the opportunity to visit this restaurant again, but this time for indoor dining.

My review thoughts have not changed. This is a very very good restaurant. The menu is quite eclectic, from Thai curry to steak to kebabs. I once again had the lamb kebabs, and once again they were outstanding.

The wait staff service was also very good.

Should be very high on any Carmel visitors restaurant dining list< /review>

<rating>3< /rating><text>Food ‚≠ê‚≠ê‚≠ê‚≠ê‚≠ê Service ‚≠ê‚≠ê‚≠ê
Personal Touch ‚≠ê‚≠ê

Restaurants are like love affairs. It doesn't have to be perfect, but some things will make it last.

We came from a far to visit this restaurant. We waited about 40 minutes for a table. Met Fadi, the Jordanian entrepreneur who owns the restaurant. Very pleasant.

The food was absolutely delicious. The sauces were just perfectly done, not overly creamy, just the right consistency. The food combinations were awesome.

The server didn't recommend any appetizers. Went from drinks to main course. When asked about the Ravioli special vs. the seafood pasta, he said he liked both but couldn't recommend one over the other. So I ordered both. Though the owner knew we came from a far and it was to celebrate a birthday, there was no effort to make the birthday girl's evening special.

The server only visited the table just once since the order. The owner didn't visit any tables while we were there.

We would have ordered dessert and wine had the service was better. This is where the relationship part come in. We would have gladly spent a lot more money, but went elsewhere for dessert and wine.

There was a table of 4 next to us who just had water, no dessert, but was googling where to go from there. Missed opportunity.

There are many great restaurants in Carmel. We come to Carmel often. We come for that special Carmel experience and service. I hope Fadi realizes that it's a privilege to have customers, not a privilege to eat at his restaurant. Make the customers feel amazing and they will return even if the food missed a beat that day or on that dish.

Great potential at this location and at this restaurant. Keep the kitchen staff, but change the attitude, spend more time taking care of your customers. Get to know them. They will come back. They will spend more money per check. They will be more forgiving.</text><pics>[{'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipOP8hkMQFYDV2Us9G96c0nZYW4uTiiMxQQZN2y7=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': < Name>

< Time>
1567440366182</Time>
< rate>
1< /rate>
< Text>
I was expecting at least a solid 3 in dining experience, based on the overall 4.6 rating (restaurant ratings in and around Monterey seem to be artificially inflated, for some reason).

The servers were friendly, but did forget to put our appetizer order in. We got the chicken pesto pasta and the beef stroganoff. Both dishes were severely lacking in meat portions, so we ended up paying about $22 - $24 for a bowl of noodles. The meals were relatively bland and tasteless. I think this restaurant uses its location, rather than food quality, to attract customers.

The chicken pesto pasta was greasy and oily for some reason. The chicken was not great.

The beef stroganoff was the saddest thing we received. There were 5 tiny pieces of beef in a huge bowl of noodles. They advertised mushrooms in this recipe, but we found no mushrooms in the bowl. They advertise this as Russian beef stroganoff. What they neglect to mention is this is the wartime rationed meat version of Russian beef stroganoff.

Overall, we were extremely disappointed and will not be back. I don't know what's up with the 5 star reviews, but we certainly did not have a great experience. I believe just about any restaurant in the Barnyard shopping center is superior, so I recommend you go there instead.</Text>

Surabhi Vijay< /Name>
<date>1478418648088<//date><rating>2</rating>< text>
Pretty place for sure, but without being treated right, it's hard to appreciate it.

We were seated by an uncomfortable corner of the patio right next to where the waiters constantly walk past. That was okay, since we could've chosen to change. Once our waiter appeared, he asks us 3 questions stereotyping us, mechanically and unthinkingly. After his "revealing questions", it is soon exposed within seconds of being seated that we are vegetarians. Again, too soon and too mechanically, he gives us 3 quick options that are the only ones available to us and to let him know. Waiter quickly exits the scene.

We wonder for a few minutes on what that was and decide that this is not the experience we want to give our money for. And thus we make our exit too.</text>
